<p class="kt-adv-heading52_620299-c9 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_620299-c9">Welcome to Hike Cook Share</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_3b2a9c-a1 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_3b2a9c-a1">I’m so happy you’re here! I’m a mama to three little ones, all under 5, and life is beautifully chaotic, alongside my talented chef husband who keeps the meals fancy while I chase toddlers and try to remember where I left my coffee- ha!</p>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column52_a9d790-19"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading52_199cdd-70 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-4-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_199cdd-70">About</h1>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading52_f2eeaf-4c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_f2eeaf-4c">I’m&nbsp;<em>Trisha</em>—Food, Family, and Simple Living</h2>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading52_84a7f3-24 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_84a7f3-24"> I&#8217;m so glad you&#8217;re here!</h3>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_936526-41 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_936526-41">Our kitchen is the heart of our home, and everyone in the family gets involved—even my little sous chefs! It’s incredible to watch how much they’ve learned.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_f514a7-c1 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_f514a7-c1">While busy creating whole food desserts, I’m behind the lens, capturing the special moments.</p>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column52_407686-b0"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h6 class="kt-adv-heading52_f84387-d0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_f84387-d0"><strong>How my story began</strong></h6>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_f76fa3-e3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_f76fa3-e3">Hey there! I’m so glad you’re here </p>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading52_ef736a-6b wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_ef736a-6b">If you’ve been following along since the beginning, I’m sending you a big heartfelt thank you. </h3>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_882d8e-d9 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_882d8e-d9">A little corner of the internet that brings together all my passions in one cozy, caramel-oat-filled place.</p>



<p> What started as <a href="https://hikecookshare.com/starting-a-mom-blog/" data-type="link" data-id="https://hikecookshare.com/starting-a-mom-blog/">starting a mom blog</a> back in 2022 has evolved into a lifestyle blog I’m truly proud of.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_1ebe37-75 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_1ebe37-75">It all started as a fun little hobby — sharing everyday moments, healthy toddler snacks on the go, <a href="https://hikecookshare.com/last-minute-dinner-recipes/" data-type="link" data-id="https://hikecookshare.com/last-minute-dinner-recipes/">last minute dinner recipes</a>-to <a href="https://hikecookshare.com/tips-and-tricks-in-kitchen/" data-type="link" data-id="https://hikecookshare.com/tips-and-tricks-in-kitchen/">minimalist kitchen tools</a> before I knew it, this space started growing into something so much more.</p>



<p>Along side sharing the best recipes, Here, I’ll be sharing everything from my journey of <a href="https://hikecookshare.com/shop-my-favorites/" data-type="link" data-id="https://hikecookshare.com/shop-my-favorites/">making money with Amazon</a> to creating a how to blog course, along with all the things our family loves — like homeschooling ideas for toddlers, hikes with toddlers, and dreams of building a full-blown <a href="https://hikecookshare.com/things-to-do-in-asheville-nc-this-weekend/" data-type="link" data-id="https://hikecookshare.com/things-to-do-in-asheville-nc-this-weekend/">family adventure blog</a>.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_52ca8b-ea wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_52ca8b-ea"> I especially love connecting with other RV families and offering helpful tips like <a href="https://hikecookshare.com/rv-must-haves-for-beginners/" data-type="link" data-id="https://hikecookshare.com/rv-must-haves-for-beginners/">RV must haves for beginners</a> — because let’s be real, figuring it all out takes time!</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_f33f78-7b wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_f33f78-7b"> But the real heart of it all? <strong>Food</strong>. My husband (aka my coworker and chef!) creates delicious meals, and I pour my love into desserts—especially anything with chocolate, because I just LOVE the sweet things. </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_699b07-26 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_699b07-26">Together we built our food blog and made it our creative home. </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_a20485-e2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_a20485-e2">Between blogging full time, being a mama to two toddlers and working a full-time job, I knew I needed help—so teaming up with my husband was the best decision. </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading52_33977a-93 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_33977a-93">Thanks for being here in this happy space where I share real life, favorite finds, and everything in between!</p>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading52_3c60f3-ba wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-5-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading52_3c60f3-ba">xx Trisha</h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>
